The nose behind this fragrance is Olivier Cresp. Top notes are Grapefruit, Bergamot and Pink Pepper; middle notes are Water Notes, Lavender and Cardamom; base notes are White Musk, White Woods, Cashmere Wood and Oakmoss. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Montblanc announces Legend Spirit for 2016 as a new version of the original Legend from 2011 with the slogan "Follow Your Spirit." The original fragrance symbolizes timeless elegance and classicism; Legend Intense from 2013 is its night version; and the new edition is announced as the ultimate timeless and cool scent.</p>

<p>Its aromatic - woody composition begins with a vibrant and refreshing blend of bergamot, pink pepper and grapefruit. A cool aquatic accord rules the heart which is mixed with aromatic tones of lavender and cardamom. The base ends with trendy blonde woods, cashmere, white musk and oak moss.</p>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1946008">ayywolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 13:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought a 100 ml tester bottle for like €40 for the sole purpose of using it as a gym scent. My transition to more complex, niche level fragrances definitely created a need for a freshie and I couldn't have chosen a better fragrance, since I didn't want to spend too much on it. It's generic and mass appealing for sure, but it does have a modern aquatic take on the critrus, lavander DNA. It's refreshing and works well for daytime wear. I think the longevity is perfect for gym or just casual use, as it fades after 3-4 hours depending on how much you apply. As for its price, it was definitely worth it, I do believe you can find it for even cheaper. Bottle and cap are surprisingly good quality, atomizer is really decent, so it doesn't feel cheap. I would recommend this one over any no-name knock-off cheap garbage you find at the chemist. Considering the price and the versatility, I think it's pretty solid.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2313533"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2313533#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313244" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; When I first got this it was definitely more citrusy . It leaned citrus fresh aquatic with a sweet undertone. Loved it. I have now had the bottle for a bout a year and it has definitely gone through a profile change . I noticed the maturation change after about 4 months .It still has a citrus scent but I feel a little more sweet grapefruit/orange /lemon has come out. It's not sharp but has a sweeter tone to it now . It does give off some bubble gum vibes for sure. Like a sweet citrus aqua bubble gum with a speck of lavender. It's a sweet freshie. The base notes are pretty spot on as well. It does remind me of Invictus. Especially Invictus Parfum. I can see this being a bit too sweet for some. But I think it smells great. It can be worn day or night and just about any season.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2260676"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2260676#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260637" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2176447">nastytrigger</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 19:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First fresh/clean scent I bought. I tried YSL Y first, but hadn’t saved up enough to buy so went with Legend Spirit first. I have since replaced Legend Spirit with YSL Y EDT and EDP. I prefer the EDT Y over the two.<br />
<br />
Comparing other similar frags, I prefer Legend Spirit over Invictus, Hawas, and a few English Laundry’s that smell similar. Montblanc wise, I much prefer Explorer and Individuel over Legend Spirit.<br />
<br />
For a freshie, it projects pretty well. Lasts multiple hours on me usually. I know it’s meant to be sweet, but it’s overly sweet. I’m 40 years old and it seems almost sickeningly sweet. I think that’s why I prefer YSL Y, and Eros even, as they seem smoother/tamer in their sweetness.<br />
<br />
Price is great. Discounters have 100ml for $40 on Legend Spirit. Can even possibly find at your local TJ Maxx, Burlington, or Ross. My first bottle was a tiny travel size from Ross, 4.5ml. Was a good way to try before getting a bigger bottle. I’ve since seen it at Ulta as a tester.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2258935"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2258935#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2256121" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I mean that's the best way to describe this juice honestly... I don't necessarily mean that as a bad thing either, I happen to like the smell. I don't think this scent would offend anyone it's really mass appealing. Once upon a time it was very hyped. Especially by Jeremy Fragrance, but for under $40 for a 100ML you can't really go wrong here. It's the literal definition of a dumb reach grab and go fragrance. The performance isn't the best but something you can just keep spraying for the hell of it. I would wear this to the gym or to run errands perhaps. For the dumb reach cheap category this is a banger and it could be a decent pickup for anyone getting started in their fragrance journey. <br />
<br />
7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2246934"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2246934#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2246918" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2246918" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WhiffMeister"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2170654"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2170654.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WhiffMeister" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Guerlain/Cuir-Intense-96469.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.96469.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cuir Intense"title="Cuir Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2246918ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2246918" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2170654">WhiffMeister</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-12">08/12/24 11:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I read a Marie Claire article that pitched the question of what makes a contemporary classic perfume to renowned perfumers, including Cresp. Cresp highlighted that there must be some familiar facet that people get; add to that some pleasing innovation and you're doing well. <br />
<br />
To me, the familiar facet is deodorant (and, somehow, Legend OG). I am far too novice to say with authority what the innovation might be in an objective sense, but to me it's largely in the quality of fragrance. Blending, ingredients, other thingsss 👀... when have you ever smelled a deodorant made to the standard of perfume? It feels novel and quite fun.<br />
<br />
The initial, intact deo whole spreads out into a juicy aquatic citrus, over creamy white florals and delicate, powdery musk and woods. In dry conditions I find it lands somewhwere dry and powdery, wheras if I'm sweaty the juicy citrus, aquatic and creamy notes stay at the fore.<br />
<br />
Thus I feel there are three main contrasting facets that play sequencially: citrus - aquatic &gt; creamy - silky &gt; powdery - woody<br />
<br />
That whole package feels new and familiar to me.<br />
<br />
Longevity and sillage is really good on my skin, thanks in part to the supersoaker spray nozle (I don't think "atomiser" is apt here).<br />
<br />
Suitability: anything where you want to smell fresh and unimposing for all day. It is not sexy, obnoxious or distinctive and would be ideal for someone working in service or healthcare for example. I wore it to a funeral recently because it was not an occassion that was about me at all.<br />
<br />
For the gym it's fine, but I prefer something drier. The creaminess with high heat and sweat isn't ideal. Same goes for really hot weather. Not a date fragrance at all.<br />
<br />
Deodorant but better. The price point is dead on. I think it's expert, useful, unperfumey perfume. A strong like, an eye-opener and not quite a love for me.<br />
<br />
Hope this review helps you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2246918"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2246918#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2245627" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's similar to the OG Paco rabanne Invictus in the scent profile but definitely not in the cloning side of things, it's inspired by it.<br />
<br />
The note breakdown shows its mostly watery notes, grapefruit and lavender, I don't know but for me this fragrance smells PURELY like an expensive deodorant (white musk with light pepper and bubblegum-ish undertones) which makes it perfect for sports or wearing it indoor to feel fresh and know you smell good rather than the sweaty dudes out there. <br />
<br />
Honestly its a love or hate type of fragrance, some people hate the smell of deodorant in a fragrance, some will find it really sexy. <br />
<br />
On my skin it lasts 3-4hrs depending on how much I spray it, the occasions used for this cologne makes the moderate longevity be pretty appropriate. <br />
<br />
The bottle looks cute, portable and resistent and the atomizer is alright<br />
<br />
Montblanc Legend Spirit: good value, expensive sharp deodorant gym only fragrance, begginer friendly warm weather signature. 7.25/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The drawback is that the projection and longevity on the skin are lacklustre, so it requires refreshing throughout the day. It is a fantastic and inexpensive choice for work and the gym.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2209721"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2209721#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2208952" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Overal rating: 5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2175847"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2175847#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2175678" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
great alternative to Invictus</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2165959"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2165959#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2165350" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2165350" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ivanthegreat"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094715"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ivanthegreat" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2165350ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2165350" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094715">ivanthegreat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-23">05/23/24 09:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me throw some adjectives out to describe this fragrance: bright, fresh, uplifting, sunny, masculine, slightly woody<br />
<br />
Waking up bright and early and throwing some of this on to start the day is a pastime of mine. The scent somehow manages to make me feel awake and refreshed. It’s mass appealing and suitable for absolutely any age, any season, and any occasion. I wore this year-round when I was in high school and it’s also my dad’s signature scent as a man in his 40’s. So it can really be pulled off by anyone. It’s such a beautiful and pleasant scent, and others will enjoy it too even though it might not solicit rave compliments. <br />
<br />
The performance leaves a little to be desired. It lasts me through half a work day, which isn’t bad but isn’t great either. Projection is really only there when it’s first sprayed, after that it sits at most a couple inches away from your skin. Even when I spray it on, it feels watery on my skin. I’m not sure what the exact oil concentration is but I’m sure it’s quite low.<br />
<br />
Final note: if a beast mode reformulation came out, I’d probably make it my signature scent even over the niche fragrances in my collection that are 10x the price. Yes it is mass appealing. <br />
But it is done soo right ✅ <br />
And it is priced right <br />
<br />
<br />
And God forbid something being mass appealing and pleasant to most noses 👃 because that means it isnt unique enough. <br />
<br />
But this is such an easy wear and women fookin love it. <br />
<br />

<br />

<br />

<br />

<br />

-Update. This really is a hilarious fragrance in a sense that I love it so much but the current formulation's performance is arguably one of the worst on the market lol. It's a much lighter version of Legend EDT which is a favourite mens fragrance of mine (as well as the EDP). <br />
It's refreshing and transparent but not a straight up freshie/aquatic/after shower scent. It's a good summer or all-year daytime scent for men who would otherwise go for something deeper or spicier but don't want to blast people away. Also great for work, gym, or any occasion where you need something safe, inoffensive, but still to smell good, classy and very respectable. <br />
Spirit will still draw people in with that enticing DNA of Legend. I see clearly the type of men who would wear this and suit this (those who wish to be quietly successful, mind their business, etc, and are not at all a fragile masculinity type who need to impress), yet I can also say this wouldn't necessarily disagree with anyone either!  Safe blind buy if you love Legend EDT or EDP and need the lighter version.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2093992"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2093992#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2089709" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Edit: 4 pm and I still smell it. I think yall are going nose blind. Personally, if yall sprayed the fragrances further away from ur nose, then you would enjoy a longer lasting, more pleasant wearing experience. I sprayed this today, 6 sprays total, on the wrist, the forearm and elbow crease, same places i always spray. Never spray neck area anymore. My 2 cents.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2087697"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2087697#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2087185" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1421242">waymonbrown84</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-26">02/26/24 07:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Legend Spirit is nice. I've underestimated this fragrance at times thinking of it as being too simple while very pleasant smelling. I'm now on my second bottle - a 1.7 oz after going through a 1 oz. quickly a couple of Summer's ago, thinking that it was too light and going spray crazy. <br />
<br />
I smell sexy to myself when I wear this (pause). I'll keep this review fairly simple. <br />
<br />
-It smells very good.<br />
-The atomizer is very good.<br />
-It's a fantastic bargain at discounters online.<br />
-It performs in cool weather.<br />
-You'll smell clean and get compliments.<br />
-You can make it a signature scent if you're a very hygienic guy as the fragrance easily compliments a generally clean man. <br />
-It can actually choke you out a little if you spray too much in the front of your neck between the white musk and oakmoss.<br />
-You'll feel confident wearing it and love the way that you smell.<br />
-It's simple but not basic, (think streamlined and linear very well done.)<br />
- It's very aromatic<br />
- It's there even when you can't tell for about 5 hours<br />
- 3 or 4 sprays will be a complimentary way to wear this.<br />
- Nice lavender scent that's not really soapy, rather clean-balanced sweet and somewhat creamy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2074576"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2074576#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2073323" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I do think it smells a bit cheap, almost smells like you aren’t wearing cologne, but just had your clothes freshly washed. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2063729" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Faabz"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1934938"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1934938.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Faabz" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2063729ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2063729" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1934938">Faabz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-15">02/15/24 22:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To appreciate Legend Spirit you have to understand that this is a freshie blended by the arguable goat of freshies, Oliver Cresp. You also have to understand that it resembles the smell of deodorant/fresh laundry, I personally like to smell clean so I love it but it definitely won't be for everyone.<br />
<br />
With that said, this is definitely more complex than a deodorant or laundry scent. The citrus/lavender in the opening is lovely and balanced. To me the dry down reminds of BDC if you took out all the amber notes. Performance is decent, it doesn't project a ton but it lasts.<br />
<br />
 I love how underrated this frag is and I really disagree with reviewers that say it smells cheap. If you came here looking for oud, leather, tobacco, amber, booze etc you're gonna be disappointed, but if you're looking to smell fresh out the shower with clean clothes I would definitely recommend this inexpensive gem.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1961559">SmellMasterBoss</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-02">02/02/24 07:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Invictus, but better in every way other than longevity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2049867"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2049867#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2049382" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2049382" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Carlitos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1071323.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Carlitos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2049382ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2049382" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323">Carlitos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-01">02/01/24 17:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THE FRESH AND LIGHT AQUATIC SPIRIT<br />
<br />
As per the Cambridge English Dictionary, "Spirit" may stand for " a particular way of feeling".<br />
The Legend Spirit aims to give you a cheerful mood and refresh your senses in Spring and Summer hot days, or tropical vacations. And it is quite successful at it.<br />
Designed in the trails of scents like Invictus Aqua, Rasasi Hawas or Carven l'Eau Intense, it works like a magician when you are either at the seaside, in the gym, or even in the hot ambience of a club.<br />
You start this Legend journey with a precious and refreshing grapefruit well supported by bergamot and the inevitable pink pepper. The coolness evolves for a refreshing aqueous, dewy note, providing you the sought-after freshness. The mossy and musky bottom wood notes that follow will try against all odds to retain some of that coolness and moisture during the drydown. Unfortunately, the drydown does not last long, but you can always respray this cool Spirit at your own will.<br />
The fragrance is quite alluring and a big success with the gentle gender. It's quite a seductive quality scent in the line of many designer expensive EDTs.<br />
Let's see how we may score this Legendary Spirit:<br />
___ ___ ___ ___ ___ ___ ___<br />
Scent Opening: 8.5 (nice, seductive and cool)<br />
Scent Dry Down: 7.5 (very nice and alluring, but so faint...)<br />
Longevity: 6.75 (3 good sprays may last up to 4~5 hours)<br />
Sillage: 6.5 (3 feet at its peak with 3 heavy sprays and 1~1.5 hours of shy projection)<br />
Uniqueness: 6.5 (3.5 points taken due to its similarity with Invictus Aqua, Legend, Invictus, Carven l'Eau Intense, Zara Teahupoo and Dark Crude, Dunhill Icon Racing, Cartier Pasha Noir Sport, Rasasi Hawas, Armaf Aura, Kelsey Berwin Zeus, Versace Man Eau Fraiche, King of Seduction, Blu di Roma Uomo, Aqva Pour Homme Marine, Terre d'Hermes Eau Tres Fraiche, Brit Splash, Aques Estiara, ... of course I am not comparing neither price nor performance; many of the fragrances I mentioned were released after Legend Spirit, so actually they are copying it..)<br />
Wearability: 8.0 (very easy to wear but avoid cold weather)<br />
Versatility: 8.5 ("all around" versatile fragrance provided it's not cold. Reigning king as a fragrance for the beach, work out, summer city tourism, esplanade "dolce far niente" and for an open air club.)<br />
Compliments: 9.0 (This fragrance it's a compliment magnet but don't forget to respray)<br />
Quality: 8.5 (Above average quality, quality ingredients, nice flask, nice cap, nice sprayer; If it wouldn't be for the performance issues, I would rate it with a 10.0)<br />
Presentation: 9.0 (no faults, simple but elegant, the best-looking bottle of all the aquatic scents I mentioned earlier and a lot more pretty than the Invictus tacky flask)<br />
Price: 8.0 (100 ml non-tester for €31, so half of Invictus Aqua price, but 2.5 times the price of Zara Teahupoo or Dark Crude; The price is slowly coming down in the web distributors; Recently I bought a 2nd flask for €20,00 on sale).<br />
___ ___ ___ ___ ___ ___ ___<br />
Overall rating: 7.89/10.0<br />
- between 7 and 8 =above average;<br />
- between 8 and 9 = recommended;<br />
- bigger than 9 = don't miss it;<br />
<br />
My opinion: If you want a very agreeable, fresh, alluring scent, that you may use in the gym or beach, and that you may wear together or in place of Invictus Aqua 2016, by no means go ahead and buy it. It became an inexpensive fragrance and you can safely purchase it blindly. Spirit price dropped to the same level as Legend Chrome (or even cheaper), and is slowly raising its sales again.<br />
<br />
Music: Beach Boys - "Surfin USA"</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="2049382"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=2049382#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2045685" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its almost overpowering if you're not careful with the sprays.  Good but sorta one note with the strong soapy citrus - yeah drydown is ok with some slight woodsy/muskyness, but not much. The citrus pop at the start is really fun, I don't get the pink peppercorn on myself but I do get about 10-15 minutes of great grapefruit-bergamot brightness! As it dries down I love the much more classic warmth and cuddliness the woods, oakmoss, lavender, and musk give this. The aquatic and water notes are individually discernable to me, but lift this out of something that is just heavy with all of the above and it keeps that edge of brightness the citrus open had. <br />
Strong sillage on me, arms length easily for at least 4 hours, and lasts 8 or more total. Leans masculine but if you find yourself drawn to lavender or oakmoss unisex scents, I find this very wearable as someone who isn't overtly masculine presenting!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
Scent: 7/10<br />
Longevity: 5/10<br />
Projection: 4/10<br />
Bottle: 8/10<br />
Value for money: 7/10<br />
Overall: 6.2/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1983597"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1983597#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1980946" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I like this because everything doesn't need to be complex but just need to do one job. And for $20 this fragrance gets that one job done.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1980946"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1980946#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1967205" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1763282">TwoWheelAUS</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-02">11/02/23 19:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Great laundry fresh, masculine, clean fragrance. The opening is average, this is where you can tell it's a value oriented fragrance. The top notes come off quite synthetic and sharp, it's not bad, it's just average. The dry down after 45 minutes is where this really shines to my nose. It gets a LOT smoother, velvety, still sweet. Very well rounded dry down. The performance is also decent, I get 5-7 hours of moderately strong scent on skin, it's not one of those time waster fragrances you can barely smell after 2 hours. <br />
<br />
This is a perfect gift fragrance for a man who doesn't have much of a collection, they will get use out of it. But personally in 2023 I think there are more interesting freshie alternatives in this price range or below (this is currently $70 in Aus, $45 USD) such as Armaf Club De Nuit Sillage or Milestone, even Lattafa Fakhar Black.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
Very well blended, there's not too much of any ingredient, but you can enjoy them all, from the sparkling start, to the elegant, fresh and masculine next 5-6 hours, after that, aprox 2 hours of skin scent.<br />
<br />
The citrus with water notes and lavender makes it very fresh, but aromatic; cardamom gives you a little of spicy sweetness, while musk balanced it with a softness note. The woody base adds the masculine note.<br />
<br />
The longevity is very good to be a Montblanc, a lot much better than Starwalker, Presence, Individuel, etc. I have read that some people suffer nose blinding or anosmia with this one, so be careful, don't overspray it. I recommend to do a test, when you don't get any smell, ask someone if they still can smell your perfume.<br />
<br />
By the way, I got compliments from ladies, they love it and a guy from the office asked me what I was wearing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1965932"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1965932#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1962510" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's the sort of scent I often wore to high school, and that was long ago and far away. Aquatics all smell light and fresh for a few minutes. Most go downhill quickly. All of the "reminds me of" listed are pretty close, but you could really cite any of thirty aquatic freshies for the list. Smelled one you've pretty much smelled them all. This one does hold on longer than many I've tried, actually smells way better after it dries down, with a kind of barbershop shave cream warmness many freshies don't feature. And it's being sold at a fair price whereas Invictus Aqua is a complete ripoff at 3x the cost. For shame Paco!<br />
<br />
I also have purchased Rasasi Hawas. I'm not really a huge fan of it either, but I do like it a bit better as for $15 more it has actual balls. Yeah, it's synthetic, but name anything at this price point that isn't. We'll wait. <br />
<br />
Personally, having purchased and trialed a few dozen scents in this category, I'm kinda done with them, and probably will repurchase none. For me this one is a keeper, at least for now. Most are already boxed up for the men's shelter Christmas shipment.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1962510"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1962510#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1960818" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1952620" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jsk03"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1408672"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="jsk03" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1952620ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1952620" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1408672">jsk03</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-15">10/15/23 14:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is my go-to for daytime wear. In essence, it's an EDT that gives off a deodorant-like scent with good longevity.<br />
<br />
Upon application on my skin, it begins with refreshing citrus and aquatic notes, at times stays for an extended period. Occasionally, subtle lavender notes make an appearance. As it dries down, it transforms into a blend of mossy and cashmere notes that remain detectable. Even after a few washes, the mossy note lingers on some materials.<br />
<br />
In terms of performance, it's decent. I primarily use it for activities like the gym and outdoors. I'd advise against wearing this fragrance in colder weather, as its strong citrus and aldehyde elements have triggered sneezing for me. To sum it up, it's a worthy substitute for deodorant.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1952620"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1952620#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1952425" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1942087" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="pilotdc"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1587795"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1587795.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="pilotdc" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1942087ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1942087" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1587795">pilotdc</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-01">10/01/23 19:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a travel size of MBLS cuz I really like the drydown. While the sweet, fruity opening is similar to Invictus and Hawas, Legend Spirit dries down to something a little more manly with the wood, cardamom, and musk while retaining some of it's original sweetness. <br />
It's good. I just wish it performed better. But I think I'll get better performance out of it when I'm in hotter and humider climates.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1942087"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1942087#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1938133" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1938133" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TipTopNotes"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1538832"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1538832.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TipTopNotes" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1938133ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1938133" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1538832">TipTopNotes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-26">09/26/23 19:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells like a thick, fresh, and sweet bubblegum with a very fuzzy edge to it (and I do mean edge). Without being insulting, I really do think Legend Spirit smells like an aerosol air freshener or a spray deodorant; it's sharp up top and rough-around-the-edges. Meanwhile, the lavender and musk notes definitely add a laundry detergent or dryer-sheet facet to the scent. The scent is a solid 7/10 when it all comes together to create the big scent-picture of pink bubblegum. However, sometimes I catch whiffs where the grapefruit really pops out, creating a wonderfully sweet, airy blast of refreshing citrus. When this happens, the scent shoots up to an impressive 9/10. These moments are fleeting however, and most of the time it smells like spray-can bubblegum.<br />
<br />
As for performance, it does pretty well. I picked up modest whiffs sprayed on my chest for 6 hours and it lasted the rest of the time I was awake as a skin scent. Be warned, this fragrance is easy to go noseblind to if sprayed close to the nose. It easily overwhelms and clogs the nasal passages with its thick but sharp aroma if you're not careful.<br />
<br />
Montblanc Legend Spirit is a decent fragrance for the price, and a solid one at discounter prices. If you're looking for a pleasing fresh and clean scent that works in the warmer parts of the year, you might want to get your nose on a sample/decant of this. If you have other fragrances that smell akin to laundry products (Prada Luna Rossa Ocean EDT, and arguably Lacoste Blanc EDT) or already have Invictus, then this might be a bit too close to justify. All things considered, I gave up my bottle because of redundancy, but I'd still give it a 7.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1938133"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1938133#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1936921" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; SUMMER ONLY...<br />
This was pure MEH, when I first bought it, but I left it for 2 years because I have far superior fragrances on my shelves. <br />
Just took it off the shelf, on a whim, being tired of the rough, harshness of Armaf and needing to feel something different...<br />
Even though this is an intimate scent, through-and-through, it still contains beautiful ingredients, that are blended extremely well, and the smell is divine.<br />
Women like this one, too.<br />
<br />
I am glad that I've since grown to appreciate this fragrance, as I'd gotten quite tired of cycling the same four scents and was in need of a shake-up.<br />
<br />
Gorgeous stuff!😍<br />
...but absolutely DISMAL longevity😬<br />
Luckily, I can carry the bottle around with me and reapply when it dissipates.<br />
This smells like Bleu De Chanel, which I don't like.<br />
The price difference is CRAZY, though!...😳</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1926374"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1926374#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1917972" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Summer, Spring, and maybe early Fall fragrance. Crowd pleaser. Fresh. A bit boring and familiar but nothing wrong with that sometimes. Underrated in my opinion. The longevity is mediocre maybe 4-5 hrs. but not bad for the price. Grapefruit, lavender, cardamom, aquatic hints then the bass notes are hints of musk and woods. Overall solid. Great value too. This is a daily driver for me. Minimum 5-6 sprays to get some good projection and longevity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1917972"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1917972#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="33443" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/993365">MrHonest</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-01">05/01/17 11:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>@TonyAKAMrClean - Seconded<br />
<br />
20% Legend, 30% Sauvage, 50% Invictus = Legend Spirit. That is EXACTLY what I thought when wearing this.<br />
<br />
And while I must say that I REALLY do enjoy the opening, that initial citrusy fruitiness dissipates rather quickly and soon transforms into a slightly cloying, slightly spicy-musky sweetness that very obviously mirrors Invictus, but with an overall shower-gel vibe.<br />
<br />
In fact, the first time I smelled this in Sephora, I was like "Oooo Dove+care shower gel!" It's definitely a familiar smell, but it just turns too sweet on my skin after a while - just like Legend Intense, which smells exactly like AXE Apollo.<br />
<br />
Still, the juice is actually blended quite well and the longevity on me is above average. The compliment factor is also unsurprisingly high, given that the masses tend to prefer sweet-freshies with a slight masculine edge. Starwalker is my signature scent, so you'll never hear any Mont Blanc hate coming from me. It's a solid house IMO, particularly for the budget conscious.<br />
<br />
So yeah, that's it. If you enjoy Invictus and its flankers, this is probably a better overall scent. It's sweet, fresh, spicy and well recieved, especially in the higher heat. I won't be buying a bottle, but if you're looking for that one generic that fits most categories (like BDC), then this just might float your boat. Big time.<br />
<br />
Scent - 6.5/10<br />
Longevity - 8/10<br />
Projection - 8/10<br />
Compliment factor - 8/10<br />
Overall - 7.5/10 - A sweetie out of the shower.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="818423"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=818423#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent961079" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Granted this effect could be purely attributable to my own personal biology but the metallic note is common to all genomes!<br />
<br />
Sadly this peforms like a strong body wash in reality and then downgrades itself to a different summer body wash after 30 minutes...<br />
<br />
Not a unique enough standout concoction to warrant the 'fragrance" label I'm afraid - more suited to a spray on deoderant really.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; And get 2018 IA instead.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="1275185"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=1275185#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent692971" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Makes no real impression, has no "WOW!" factor. It has a scent, but it's almost indistinguishable from a freshly-laundered shirt. I suppose that's the musk in it. <br />
<br />
Is it "safe for work?" Sure. If your goal is to get your co-workers to yawn in your face, this is your frag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33443"comment_id="692971"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Legend-Spirit-33443.html?ccid=692971#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent945329" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
